--- Commit Message ---
LU-9868 llite: use d_splice_alias for directories.

In the Linux dcache a directory only ever has one dentry,
so d_splice_alias() can be used by ll_splice_alias() for directories.
It will find the one dentry whether it is DCACHE_DISCONNECTED or
IS_ROOT() or d_lustre_invalid().
Separating out the directories from non-directories will allow us
to simplify the non-directory code.

Linux-commit: e9d4f0b9f55920821845b8e063ed593422c18d8a
Linux-commit: 1d6e65bedf5878c8dd5b089d3f034b619bbb8a77

Signed-off-by: NeilBrown <neil@brown.name>
Signed-off-by: Greg Kroah-Hartman <gregkh@linuxfoundation.org>
Change-Id: If80a02b77c4fc62cdb90e86cdb8a0f9eba21193b

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2024-03-21 14:36:39.000000000) ---
Patch Set 7:

> We have TWO dentries was the same FID. For example OBF both $MOUNT/.lustre/fid and $MOUNT/.lustre/fid/[OBF_FID] have the same FID. If the path is $MOUNT/.lustre/fid that is okay but $MOUNT/.lustre/fid/[OBF_FID] is not since its equal to its parent. So in that case if both parent is OBF and child is OBF we pick the parent.

probably we shouldn't let open $MOUNT/.lustre/fid/[OBF_FID] and return an error instead?

--- Message (James Simmons, 2024-03-21 15:17:15.000000000) ---
Patch Set 7:

Then sanity 233 test would fail. This behavior is baked into the Lustre API. So we have to support it but at the same time not break the dcache.

--- Message (Neil Brown, 2024-03-26 22:44:03.000000000) ---
Patch Set 11:

I don't think we should be using d_real() for this.

When a lookup in .lustre/fid finds with .lustre or .lustre/fid, it should just return that dentry.
If it finds any other directory inode, it should probably use exportfs_decode_fh_raw() to find or create the dentry.

--- Message (James Simmons, 2024-03-26 23:09:35.000000000) ---
Patch Set 12:

Actually using d_real helps in several other areas of the code in that it retrieves the correct root directory as a side affect. For example in ll_dir_ioctl() we have file_dentry() which will return the root for a fileset when setting the default layout for the root directory. I suspect for the special .lustre and .lustre/fid case it will resolve
other brokeness as well as a side effect of this change.
